(function () {
  'use strict';

  var APP = window.__APP_INIT__ || {};

  var DEFAULTS = {
    maxNoteLength: 50000,
    searchDebounce: 300,
    apiBase: '/api'
  };

  var ACCOUNT_PREFERENCES_API = DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/account/preferences';

  // Settings helpers.

  function mergeFormData(target, source) {
    if (!source || typeof source !== 'object') return target;
    var keys = Object.keys(source);
    for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
      var k = keys[i];
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(source, k)) continue;
      if (typeof source[k] === 'object' && source[k] !== null) continue;
      target[k] = source[k];
    }
    return target;
  }

  function getOwnString(obj, key, fallback) {
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string') {
      return obj[key];
    }
    return fallback;
  }

  function getOwnArray(obj, key) {
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) && Array.isArray(obj[key])) {
      return obj[key];
    }
    return [];
  }

  // Hash-based appearance preferences.

  function setNestedValue(obj, path, value) {
    var keys = path.replace(/\]/g, '').split('[');
    var current = obj;
    for (var i = 0; i < keys.length - 1; i++) {
      var k = keys[i];
      if (k === '__proto__') return;
      if (
        current[k] == null ||
        (typeof current[k] !== 'object' && typeof current[k] !== 'function')
      ) {
        current[k] = {};
      }
      current = current[k];
    }
    var last = keys[keys.length - 1];
    if (last !== '__proto__') {
      current[last] = value;
    }
  }

  function parseThemeParams() {
    var hash = location.hash;
    if (!hash || hash.length < 2) return;
    var raw = hash.substring(1);
    var pairs = raw.split('&');
    var result = {};

    for (var i = 0; i < pairs.length; i++) {
      var idx = pairs[i].indexOf('=');
      if (idx === -1) continue;
      try {
        var key = decodeURIComponent(pairs[i].substring(0, idx));
        var val = decodeURIComponent(pairs[i].substring(idx + 1));
        setNestedValue(result, key, val);
      } catch (e) {
        continue;
      }
    }

    if (result.theme)  APP.theme  = result.theme;
    if (result.font)   document.body.style.fontFamily = result.font;
    if (result.accent) document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent', result.accent);
    if (result.bg)     document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--bg-primary', result.bg);
  }

  // Remote layout manifest.

  function applyRemoteProfile(profile) {
    if (!profile || typeof profile !== 'object') return;

    if (typeof profile.renderMode === 'string') {
      APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode;
    }

    if (Array.isArray(profile.widgetTypes)) {
      APP.widgetTypes = profile.widgetTypes
        .filter(function (value) { return typeof value === 'string'; })
        .slice(0, 8);
    }

    if (typeof profile.widgetSink === 'string') {
      APP.widgetSink = profile.widgetSink;
    }

    if (typeof profile.theme === 'string') {
      APP.theme = profile.theme;
    }
  }

  function loadPanelManifest() {
    if (typeof window.__NOTE_CONTENT__ !== 'string') {
      return Promise.resolve();
    }

    var panel  = typeof APP.panel === 'string' ? APP.panel : 'summary';
    var noteId = typeof APP.noteId === 'string' ? APP.noteId : '';
    if (!noteId) return Promise.resolve();

    var target = '/note/' + encodeURIComponent(noteId) + '/' + panel +
      '/manifest.json?note=' + encodeURIComponent(noteId);

    return fetch(target, {
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    })
      .then(function (r) {
        if (!r.ok) return null;
        return r.json();
      })
      .then(function (data) {
        if (data && data.profile) {
          applyRemoteProfile(data.profile);
        }
      })
      .catch(function () {});
  }

  // Content policies.

  function loadContentPolicies() {
    var mode = getOwnString(APP, 'renderMode', 'safe');
    return {
      allowForms:         mode === 'full',
      allowIds:           mode === 'full',
      allowDataAttrs:     mode === 'full',
      enableEnhancements: mode === 'full'
    };
  }

  // DOMPurify config.

  function getSanitizeConfig() {
    var cfg = {
      ALLOWED_TAGS: [
        'h1','h2','h3','h4','h5','h6',
        'p','br','hr',
        'b','i','u','em','strong','del','ins','sub','sup','mark',
        'a','img',
        'ul','ol','li',
        'blockquote','code','pre','kbd','samp',
        'table','caption','thead','tbody','tfoot','tr','th','td',
        'span','div',
        'figure','figcaption',
        'abbr','cite','q','small','time','var',
        'dl','dt','dd'
      ],
      ALLOWED_ATTR: [
        'href','src','alt','title',
        'class','style',
        'target','rel',
        'width','height',
        'colspan','rowspan','scope',
        'cite','datetime','lang','dir'
      ],
      ALLOW_DATA_ATTR: false
    };

    var policies = loadContentPolicies();

    if (policies.allowForms) {
      cfg.ALLOWED_TAGS = cfg.ALLOWED_TAGS.concat([
        'form','input','select','option','textarea',
        'label','fieldset','legend',
        'details','summary','dialog',
        'meter','progress','output'
      ]);
    }

    if (policies.allowIds) {
      cfg.ALLOWED_ATTR = cfg.ALLOWED_ATTR.concat([
        'id','name','value','type','placeholder',
        'for','method','action',
        'checked','selected','disabled','readonly',
        'required','pattern','autocomplete',
        'rows','cols','wrap','maxlength','minlength',
        'multiple','size','accept','list',
        'open','tabindex','role',
        'min','max','step','low','high','optimum',
        'aria-label','aria-describedby'
      ]);
    }

    if (policies.allowDataAttrs) {
      cfg.ALLOW_DATA_ATTR = true;
    }

    return cfg;
  }

  function sanitize(html) {
    if (typeof DOMPurify === 'undefined') return '';
    return DOMPurify.sanitize(html, getSanitizeConfig());
  }

  // Post-sanitisation data attribute filter.

  var UNSAFE_CONTENT_RE = /script|cookie|document|window|eval|alert|prompt|confirm|Function|fetch|XMLHttp|import|require|setTimeout|setInterval/i;

  function postSanitize(html) {
    var temp = document.createElement('div');
    temp.innerHTML = html;
    temp.querySelectorAll('*').forEach(function (el) {
      var attrs = el.attributes;
      for (var i = attrs.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        var attr = attrs[i];
        if (attr.name.indexOf('data-') === 0 && UNSAFE_CONTENT_RE.test(attr.value)) {
          el.removeAttribute(attr.name);
        }
      }
    });
    return temp.innerHTML;
  }

  // Note rendering.

  function renderNoteContent() {
    var display = document.getElementById('note-display');
    var content = window.__NOTE_CONTENT__;
    if (!display || typeof content !== 'string') return;

    var clean = sanitize(content);
    var safe  = postSanitize(clean);
    display.innerHTML = safe;

    display.querySelectorAll('a[href]').forEach(function (a) {
      if (a.hostname !== location.hostname) {
        a.setAttribute('rel', 'noopener noreferrer');
        a.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
      }
    });

    display.querySelectorAll('img').forEach(function (img) {
      img.loading = 'lazy';
      img.onerror = function () { this.style.display = 'none'; };
    });
  }

  // Inline enhancements.

  function initContentEnhancements() {
    var container = document.getElementById('note-display');
    if (!container) return;

    var observer = new MutationObserver(function () {
      processEnhancements(container);
    });
    observer.observe(container, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  }

  function processEnhancements(root) {
    var policies = loadContentPolicies();
    if (!policies.enableEnhancements) return;

    var manifestTypes = getOwnArray(APP, 'widgetTypes');
    if (!manifestTypes.length) return;

    var configEl = document.getElementById('enhance-config');
    if (!configEl) return;
    var allowedTypes = (configEl.dataset.types || '').split(',');

    root.querySelectorAll('[data-enhance]:not([data-processed])').forEach(function (el) {
      el.dataset.processed = '1';
      var type = el.dataset.enhance;
      if (allowedTypes.indexOf(type) === -1) return;
      if (manifestTypes.indexOf(type) === -1) return;

      switch (type) {
        case 'counter':
          animateCounter(el);
          break;
        case 'progress':
          animateProgress(el);
          break;
        case 'custom':
          loadCustomWidget(el);
          break;
      }
    });
  }

  function animateCounter(el) {
    var target = parseInt(el.dataset.to || '100', 10);
    var current = 0;
    var step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(target / 60));
    var timer = setInterval(function () {
      current = Math.min(current + step, target);
      el.textContent = current;
      if (current >= target) clearInterval(timer);
    }, 16);
  }

  function animateProgress(el) {
    var pct = parseInt(el.dataset.pct || '0', 10);
    el.style.width = '0%';
    el.style.transition = 'width 1s ease';
    requestAnimationFrame(function () {
      el.style.width = Math.min(pct, 100) + '%';
    });
  }

  function loadCustomWidget(el) {
    if (getOwnString(APP, 'widgetSink', 'text') !== 'script') return;

    var cfg = el.dataset.cfg;
    if (!cfg || cfg.length > 512) return;
    var s = document.createElement('script');
    s.textContent = cfg;
    document.head.appendChild(s);
  }

  // Search.

  var searchTimer = null;

  function initSearch() {
    var input   = document.getElementById('search-input');
    var results = document.getElementById('search-results');
    if (!input || !results) return;

    input.addEventListener('input', function () {
      clearTimeout(searchTimer);
      var q = this.value.trim();
      if (q.length < 2) { results.innerHTML = ''; return; }

      searchTimer = setTimeout(function () {
        fetch(DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent(q))
          .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
          .then(function (data) {
            if (!data.results || !data.results.length) {
              results.innerHTML = '<div class="no-results">No notes found</div>';
              return;
            }
            results.innerHTML = data.results.map(function (n) {
              return '<a href="/note/' + encodeURIComponent(n.id) +
                     '" class="search-result">' + escapeHtml(n.title) + '</a>';
            }).join('');
          })
          .catch(function () {
            results.innerHTML = '<div class="no-results">Search failed</div>';
          });
      }, DEFAULTS.searchDebounce);
    });
  }

  // Local note history.

  var STORAGE_KEY = 'chainnotes_my_ids';

  function getSavedIds() {
    try {
      var raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
      if (!raw) return [];
      var ids = JSON.parse(raw);
      return Array.isArray(ids) ? ids : [];
    } catch (e) {
      return [];
    }
  }

  function saveNoteId(id) {
    var ids = getSavedIds();
    if (ids.indexOf(id) === -1) {
      ids.unshift(id);
      if (ids.length > 200) ids = ids.slice(0, 200);
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(ids));
    }
  }

  function loadPrivateNotes() {
    var grid  = document.getElementById('private-notes-grid');
    var empty = document.getElementById('private-notes-empty');
    if (!grid) return;

    var ids = getSavedIds();
    if (!ids.length) return;

    fetch(DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/notes/lookup', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ ids: ids })
    })
      .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
      .then(function (data) {
        if (!data.notes) return;
        var found = data.notes.filter(function (n) { return n.found; });
        if (!found.length) return;
        if (empty) empty.style.display = 'none';
        found.forEach(function (n) {
          var a = document.createElement('a');
          a.href = '/note/' + encodeURIComponent(n.id);
          a.className = 'note-card';
          var h3 = document.createElement('h3');
          h3.textContent = n.title;
          var span = document.createElement('span');
          span.className = 'note-card-author';
          span.textContent = n.author;
          a.appendChild(h3);
          a.appendChild(span);
          grid.appendChild(a);
        });
      })
      .catch(function () {});
  }

  // Note creation.

  function initCreateForm() {
    var form   = document.getElementById('create-form');
    var result = document.getElementById('create-result');
    if (!form) return;

    form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var title   = form.querySelector('[name="title"]').value.trim();
      var content = form.querySelector('[name="content"]').value;

      if (!title || !content) {
        showResult(result, 'error', 'Title and content are required.');
        return;
      }

      fetch(DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/notes', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ title: title, content: content })
      })
        .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function (data) {
          if (data.success) {
            saveNoteId(data.id);
            showResult(result, 'success',
              'Note created! <a href="' + escapeHtml(data.url) + '">View note &rarr;</a>');
            form.reset();
            loadPrivateNotes();
          } else {
            showResult(result, 'error', data.error || 'Failed to create note.');
          }
        })
        .catch(function () {
          showResult(result, 'error', 'Network error.');
        });
    });
  }

  // Settings.

  function loadAccountPreferences() {
    var form = document.getElementById('settings-form');
    var meta = document.getElementById('settings-meta');

    return fetch(ACCOUNT_PREFERENCES_API)
      .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
      .then(function (data) {
        if (!data || !data.preferences) return;

        if (form) {
          setFieldValue(form, 'theme', data.preferences.theme);
          setFieldValue(form, 'fontSize', data.preferences.fontSize);
          setFieldValue(form, 'language', data.preferences.language);
          setFieldValue(form, 'defaultLayout', data.preferences.defaultLayout);
        }

        if (meta) {
          var presetCount = data.stats && typeof data.stats.presetCount === 'number'
            ? data.stats.presetCount
            : 0;
          meta.textContent = presetCount
            ? presetCount + ' reader preset' + (presetCount === 1 ? '' : 's') + ' synced to this account.'
            : 'Reader presets sync to this account automatically when they are created.';
        }
      })
      .catch(function () {});
  }

  function initSettingsForm() {
    var form   = document.getElementById('settings-form');
    var result = document.getElementById('settings-result');
    if (!form) return;

    form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var payload = {};
      new FormData(form).forEach(function (v, k) {
        payload[k] = isNaN(v) ? v : Number(v);
      });

      var merged = {};
      mergeFormData(merged, payload);

      fetch(ACCOUNT_PREFERENCES_API, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(merged)
      })
        .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function (data) {
          if (data.success) {
            if (data.preferences && typeof data.preferences.theme === 'string') {
              APP.theme = data.preferences.theme;
              applyTheme();
            }
            loadAccountPreferences();
            showResult(result, 'success', 'Settings saved.');
          } else {
            showResult(result, 'error', data.error || 'Failed.');
          }
        })
        .catch(function () {
          showResult(result, 'error', 'Network error.');
        });
    });
  }

  // Review request.

  function initReportButton() {
    var btn    = document.getElementById('report-btn');
    var result = document.getElementById('report-result');
    if (!btn) return;

    btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
      btn.disabled = true;
      var url = location.pathname + location.search + location.hash;

      fetch(DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/report', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ url: url })
      })
        .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function (data) {
          showResult(result, data.success || data.message ? 'success' : 'error',
            data.message || data.error);
          setTimeout(function () { btn.disabled = false; }, 10000);
        })
        .catch(function () {
          showResult(result, 'error', 'Network error.');
          btn.disabled = false;
        });
    });
  }

  // Theme.

  function applyTheme() {
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', APP.theme || 'dark');
  }

  // Utilities.

  function setFieldValue(form, name, value) {
    var field = form.querySelector('[name="' + name + '"]');
    if (!field || value == null) return;
    field.value = value;
  }

  function escapeHtml(str) {
    var d = document.createElement('div');
    d.textContent = str;
    return d.innerHTML;
  }

  function showResult(el, type, msg) {
    if (!el) return;
    el.className = 'result-msg result-' + type;
    el.innerHTML = msg;
    el.style.display = 'block';
    setTimeout(function () { el.style.display = 'none'; }, 8000);
  }

  // Init.

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async function () {
    parseThemeParams();
    await loadPanelManifest();
    applyTheme();
    initContentEnhancements();
    renderNoteContent();
    initSearch();
    initCreateForm();
    initSettingsForm();
    initReportButton();
    loadPrivateNotes();
    loadAccountPreferences();
  });
})();

import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
import base64

tree = ET.parse('/mnt/user-data/uploads/New.xml')
root = tree.getroot()

items = root.findall('.//item')
print(f'Total items: {len(items)}')
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    print(f'[{i}] {method} {status} {url[:100]}')
"

Decode key responses from New.xml
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
import base64

tree = ET.parse('/mnt/user-data/uploads/New.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

# Look at the full URLs to see panels, and decode interesting responses
for i in [3, 11, 14, 17, 20, 30, 31, 41, 42, 44, 45, 47]:
    item = items[i]
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    # decode response
    resp_el = item.find('response')
    if resp_el is not None and resp_el.get('base64') == 'true':
        try:
            resp = base64.b64decode(resp_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
        except:
            resp = resp_el.text or ''
    else:
        resp = resp_el.text if resp_el is not None else ''
    
    # Show URL and first 300 chars of response body (after headers)
    body_start = resp.find('\r\n\r\n')
    body = resp[body_start+4:body_start+500] if body_start != -1 else resp[:500]
    print(f'=== [{i}] {status} {url[-80:]}')
    print(body[:300])
    print()
"

Looking at applyRemoteProfile:

javascript
function applyRemoteProfile(profile) {
    if (!profile || typeof profile !== 'object') return;

    if (typeof profile.renderMode === 'string') {
      APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode;  // Sets to "safe"
    }
    // ...
}
And loadContentPolicies:

javascript
function loadContentPolicies() {
    var mode = getOwnString(APP, 'renderMode', 'safe');
    return {
      allowForms:         mode === 'full',
      allowIds:           mode === 'full',
      allowDataAttrs:     mode === 'full',
      enableEnhancements: mode === 'full'
    };
}
getOwnString uses hasOwnProperty, so prototype pollution on renderMode won't work.

But wait - applyRemoteProfile directly sets APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode. If we can control what the manifest returns...

But the manifests are all "safe" on the server side.

Find all manifest requests and their panels
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
import base64

tree = ET.parse('/mnt/user-data/uploads/New.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

# Find all manifest requests and show their full URLs and responses
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    if 'manifest' in url:
        status = item.findtext('status','')
        resp_el = item.find('response')
        if resp_el is not None and resp_el.get('base64') == 'true':
            resp = base64.b64decode(resp_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
        else:
            resp = resp_el.text if resp_el is not None else ''
        body_start = resp.find('\r\n\r\n')
        body = resp[body_start+4:body_start+300] if body_start != -1 else resp[:300]
        # also get request
        req_el = item.find('request')
        if req_el is not None and req_el.get('base64') == 'true':
            req = base64.b64decode(req_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
        else:
            req = req_el.text if req_el is not None else ''
        print(f'=== [{i}] {status} {url}')
        print('REQ first line:', req.split('\n')[0])
        print('RESP:', body[:200])
        print()
"

Check preferences and report endpoints

Script
All account/preferences responses are 304 Not Modified so I can't see the body. Let me get the first 200 response for it from the old XML.

But more importantly: All manifest endpoints return renderMode: "safe". The key insight I need is: how do we get renderMode: "full" on APP?

Let me re-read app.js very carefully.

The init sequence is:

javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async function () {
    parseThemeParams();           // 1. reads URL hash
    await loadPanelManifest();    // 2. fetches manifest, calls applyRemoteProfile
    applyTheme();                 // 3.
    initContentEnhancements();    // 4. sets up MutationObserver
    renderNoteContent();          // 5. renders note content
    ...
});
applyRemoteProfile sets APP.renderMode directly. If the manifest returns "safe", then APP.renderMode = "safe".

loadContentPolicies() uses getOwnString(APP, 'renderMode', 'safe') with hasOwnProperty. So APP.renderMode is checked as an own property.

Wait. What if applyRemoteProfile is called with a profile where profile.renderMode is truthy but not 'full'? That sets APP.renderMode = "safe".

What if applyRemoteProfile is NOT called at all? Then APP.renderMode is never set as own property, so getOwnString returns 'safe' as fallback.

Hmm. Is there any way to get APP.renderMode set to 'full' as an OWN property?

Only applyRemoteProfile sets APP.renderMode (as APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode). And the server always returns "safe".

Wait. What if we can make the manifest fetch return a different URL's content? The panel variable is NOT encoded in the URL construction:

javascript
var target = '/note/' + encodeURIComponent(noteId) + '/' + panel +
  '/manifest.json?note=' + encodeURIComponent(noteId);

Actually wait. Let me re-read loadContentPolicies:

javascript
function loadContentPolicies() {
    var mode = getOwnString(APP, 'renderMode', 'safe');
    return {
      allowForms:         mode === 'full',
      allowIds:           mode === 'full',
      allowDataAttrs:     mode === 'full',
      enableEnhancements: mode === 'full'
    };
}
getOwnString is called with APP. APP = window.__APP_INIT__ || {}. After applyRemoteProfile, APP.renderMode = "safe" (own property).

What if we pollute Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty? That would break Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) check!

getOwnString does:

javascript
if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string') {
    return obj[key];
}
If we set Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty to something... Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call would fail or behave differently.

But setting Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty = function() { return true; } via prototype pollution wouldn't work because Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty is already own on Object.prototype. We'd need to REPLACE it.

Actually, setNestedValue(result, 'constructor[prototype][hasOwnProperty]', 'anything') would set Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty = 'anything'. Then Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) would throw TypeError: Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call is not a function.

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/CTF.xml')
root = tree.getroot()

# Find account/preferences POST and 200 GET responses
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    if 'account/preferences' in url:
        resp_el = item.find('response')
        if resp_el is not None:
            if resp_el.get('base64') == 'true':
                resp = base64.b64decode(resp_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
            else:
                resp = resp_el.text or ''
            body_start = resp.find('\r\n\r\n')
            body = resp[body_start+4:body_start+600] if body_start != -1 else resp[:600]

                if req_el.get('base64') == 'true':

            else:
                req_body = ''

            if req_body.strip(): print('REQ:', req_body)

            print()

# Re-examine manifest URL construction — what does ?note= param actually do server-side?
# The manifest fetch URL is:

# APP = window.__APP_INIT__ -- server sets panel and noteId as OWN properties
# But what about the ?note= query param in the manifest fetch?

python3 -c "
# Analyze the manifest URL pattern
# /note/NOTEID/PANEL/manifest.json?note=NOTEID
# If server ignores path noteId and only uses ?note= query param...
# Then if we can make ?note= point to OUR note (attacker-controlled note)
# whose creator has readerPresets set, we get full mode!

# How? The noteId in ?note= comes from APP.noteId
# APP.noteId is set by server in __APP_INIT__
# We can't override it from hash since it's an OWN property on APP

# BUT: what if server uses ?note= to look up CREATOR preferences
# and the path noteId is just for routing?
# Then we need to find a way to change what ?note= sends

# Check: can we manipulate the manifest fetch via hash params?
# parseThemeParams only sets: APP.theme, body.fontFamily, --accent, --bg-primary
# None of those affect loadPanelManifest

# CONCLUSION: two scenarios
# 1. Manifest based on CREATOR prefs -> set attacker prefs, create note, done
# 2. Manifest based on VISITOR prefs -> need bot to have prefs

# For scenario 2: bot gets fresh northstar_profile cookie on first visit
# That session has empty readerPresets -> safe mode
# We can't inject into bot's session

# UNLESS: there's a way to make the bot visit a URL that sets its prefs first
# Then visit the note. But report only sends ONE URL.

print('Scenario analysis complete')
print('Key unknown: whose session does manifest endpoint use?')
print('Test: POST /api/account/preferences with readerPresets as attacker')  
print('Then check: does /note/{attackerNoteId}/summary/manifest.json return full?')
print('If YES -> creator-based prefs')
print('If NO -> visitor-based prefs, need different approach')
"

You're right to flag this. Two possible interpretations:

Scenario A — Creator-based: Manifest uses the note author's session. You set your presets → your note serves full to everyone including bot. ✅ Would work.

Scenario B — Reader-based (your point): Manifest uses the visitor's session. Bot has a fresh northstar_profile with empty presets → always gets safe. ❌ Our approach fails.

If it's Scenario B, the real attack vector shifts to prototype pollution + hash:

/note/{id}/summary#constructor[prototype][renderMode]=full&constructor[prototype][widgetTypes][0]=custom&constructor[prototype][widgetSink]=script
BUT — getOwnString uses hasOwnProperty, so APP.renderMode won't pick up prototype-polluted value...

UNLESS applyRemoteProfile runs first and sets APP.renderMode = "full" as an OWN property. That won't help either since manifest still returns safe.

The real question is: can you fetch the manifest as your own session (no IF-None-Match) after POSTing readerPresets, and does it return full?

Drop new1.xml — if you tested the POST to preferences, the response will tell us which scenario we're in.

Decode all New1.xml items fully
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET, base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/New1.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

def decode(el):
    if el is None: return ''
    if el.get('base64') == 'true': return base64.b64decode(el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    return el.text or ''

def body(s):
    i = s.find('\r\n\r\n')
    return s[i+4:] if i != -1 else s

# Show all requests/responses with full detail
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    req = decode(item.find('request'))
    resp = decode(item.find('response'))
    req_body = body(req)
    resp_body = body(resp)
    print(f'=== [{i}] {method} {status} {url}')
    if req_body.strip(): print('REQ:', req_body[:400])
    print('RESP:', resp_body[:500])
    print()
"

Check which session cookie each request uses
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET, base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/New1.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

def decode(el):
    if el is None: return ''
    if el.get('base64') == 'true': return base64.b64decode(el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    return el.text or ''

# Check cookies on ALL requests to see which session is which
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    req = decode(item.find('request'))
    # find Cookie header
    for line in req.split('\r\n'):
        if line.lower().startswith('cookie:'):
            print(f'[{i}] {method} {url[-60:]}')
            print('  Cookie:', line)
            break
"

bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET, base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/New1.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

def decode(el):
    if el is None: return ''
    if el.get('base64') == 'true': return base64.b64decode(el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    return el.text or ''

def body(s):
    i = s.find('\r\n\r\n')
    return s[i+4:] if i != -1 else s

# Critical: check chronological order by looking at timestamps if available
# and compare: [1] manifest fetch vs [5] prefs (with full preset)
# Both use same session f816...
# [5] has full presets, [1] manifest returns safe

# Check if there are any timestamps

    item = items[i]
    print(f'[{i}] time:', item.findtext('time', 'N/A'))
    print(f'    url:', item.findtext('url','')[-70:])

Critical timestamp finding:

08:52:43 [7] prefs → empty readerPresets
  ← (POST to set full presets, NOT captured)
08:54:11 [5] prefs → FULL readerPresets confirmed (presetCount:1)
08:55:34 [4] note CREATED
08:56:23 [1] manifest → still SAFE ❌
Conclusion: readerPresets have ZERO effect on manifest, regardless of creator vs visitor session. The preset is stored but the server ignores it for the manifest endpoint.

The actual attack is prototype pollution + a manifest missing renderMode.

Look at applyRemoteProfile:

js
if (typeof profile.renderMode === 'string') {
  APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode;  // only runs if own property!
}
If profile has NO own renderMode, profile.renderMode resolves via prototype chain. If we've polluted Object.prototype.renderMode = 'full' → APP.renderMode = 'full' gets set as OWN property → getOwnString finds it ✓

The two-part attack:

Part 1 — Set readerPresets WITHOUT renderMode (only widgetTypes + widgetSink):

json
{
  "readerPresets": {
    "summary": {
      "widgetTypes": ["custom"],
      "widgetSink": "script"
    }
  }
}
If the server applies your preset to the manifest profile but omits renderMode (since you didn't set it), the manifest returns {profile: {widgetTypes: ["custom"], widgetSink: "script"}} — no own renderMode.

Part 2 — Prototype pollution in the hash URL you report to bot:

/note/{id}/summary#constructor[prototype][renderMode]=full
Flow on bot's page:

parseThemeParams() → Object.prototype.renderMode = 'full'
loadPanelManifest() → manifest returns {profile: {widgetTypes:["custom"], widgetSink:"script"}} ← no renderMode
applyRemoteProfile(profile) → typeof profile.renderMode === 'string' → checks prototype → 'full' → APP.renderMode = 'full' ✓
DOMPurify allows data-attrs → widget fires → flag stolen
Test now in Burp Repeater: POST readerPresets WITHOUT renderMode, then fresh manifest fetch. Does it return {profile: {widgetTypes: ["custom"], widgetSink: "script"}} with no renderMode?

Decode key items with timestamps and cookies
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET, base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/804576bc8115ce7477895a776ca331f0.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

def decode(el):
    if el is None: return ''
    if el.get('base64') == 'true': return base64.b64decode(el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    return el.text or ''
def body(s):
    i = s.find('\r\n\r\n')
    return s[i+4:] if i != -1 else s
def cookie(s):
    for line in s.split('\r\n'):
        if line.lower().startswith('cookie:'): return line[8:].strip()
    return ''

# Focus on key items sorted by time
key = [18, 10, 4, 9, 3, 2, 0]
for i in key:
    item = items[i]
    t = item.findtext('time','')
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    req = decode(item.find('request'))
    resp = decode(item.find('response'))
    req_body = body(req)
    resp_body = body(resp)
    ck = cookie(req)
    print(f'=== [{i}] {t} | {method} {status}')
    print(f'    URL: {url[-80:]}')
    print(f'    Cookie: {ck[:60]}')
    if req_body.strip(): print(f'    REQ: {req_body[:300]}')
    print(f'    RESP: {resp_body[:400]}')
    print()
"

03:31:25 [17] GET prefs → (empty, 304 in XML but 200 in HAR with empty preset)

03:34:31 [38] GET prefs → {readerPresets: {summary: {widgetTypes: ["custom"], widgetSink: "script"}}} presetCount: 1 ← confirms the preset was stored
The manifest at [37] returns {renderMode: "safe", widgetTypes: ["counter", "progress"], widgetSink: "text"} DESPITE having a readerPreset with {widgetTypes: ["custom"], widgetSink: "script"}.

The readerPresets are being COMPLETELY IGNORED by the manifest endpoint.

The manifest hardcodes:

summary: {renderMode: "safe", widgetTypes: ["counter", "progress"], widgetSink: "text"}
print: {renderMode: "safe", widgetTypes: ["counter"], widgetSink: "text", theme: "light"}
compact: {renderMode: "safe", widgetTypes: [], widgetSink: "text"}
No matter what presets are set, the manifest returns these hardcoded values. The readerPresets field in the preferences API might be a complete red herring.

So the REAL question is: how do we get renderMode: full? And the answer can only come from:

The manifest returning a profile without renderMode (then prototype pollution on Object.prototype.renderMode kicks in for applyRemoteProfile)
Some other path
BUT WAIT: from the manifest response {renderMode: "safe", widgetTypes: ["counter", "progress"], widgetSink: "text"}, there's always an OWN renderMode: "safe" property. Prototype pollution can't override own properties.

Unless... we can manipulate the manifest URL to hit a different endpoint that returns different JSON.

Key observation: The manifest request at [37] has NO COOKIE in the request headers! The cookie is completely missing from the manifest request.

Look at the headers - there's no cookie: header. The request is made without a session cookie.

This is the key insight! The manifest request from the page's loadPanelManifest() is a fetch() call:

js
return fetch(target, {
    headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
})
This fetch() call doesn't include credentials: 'include' or any credentials option. In browsers, the default for fetch() is credentials: 'same-origin'. Wait, actually the default changed. In older specs it was 'omit', but in modern browsers (and Fetch spec) the default is 'same-origin' which includes cookies for same-origin requests.

But looking at the request - there's no cookie! So either:

The fetch is being made with credentials: 'omit'
Or the user opened the note page in incognito where they had no session cookie
Wait, but the HAR file is named after the session 804576bc8115ce7477895a776ca331f0, so it should be a logged-in session.

But look at the request headers more carefully - there's NO :authority + cookie combo. No cookie at all. But the account preferences request right before/after DO have the session cookie (since they're triggered by the page's loadAccountPreferences which also uses fetch but DOES include cookies).

Wait no - the HAR shows the prefs request at [29] with no cookie in the displayed output, but that might be because I'm checking [29] which shows empty response (304). Let me look at [38] - it does return the prefs. But [38] also doesn't show a cookie in the output...

Actually I think the issue is that the HAR captures might not include cookies in the headers (some browsers redact them for privacy). Let me look at this differently.

The critical observation is: the manifest request ETag is W/"5a-xpejJnk2niFUmVKyLj+WXoyjCw8". …

Done
Key finding from the manifest request headers — no Cookie was sent:

:authority: challenge-0426.intigriti.io
accept: application/json
sec-fetch-site: same-origin
... (no cookie header!)
And the ETag W/"5a-xpejJnk2niFUmVKyLj+WXoyjCw8" is identical across ALL captures, different note IDs, different sessions. The manifest is fully static — it never changes regardless of who visits or what prefs are set.

This means: summary/compact/print panels are hardcoded on the server, ignoring readerPresets completely.

But readerPresets MUST serve some purpose — presetCount is tracked, and the key names match panel names. The likely server logic:

known panels (summary/compact/print) → hardcoded manifest (overrides presets)
UNKNOWN panel name + user has preset[name] → returns user's preset as manifest!
The attack — use a custom panel name:

Step 1 — Set preset with a NON-STANDARD panel name:

json
POST /api/account/preferences
{
  "readerPresets": {
    "reader": {
      "renderMode": "full",
      "widgetTypes": ["custom"],
      "widgetSink": "script"
    }
  }
}
Step 2 — Test the manifest immediately:

GET /note/{id}/reader/manifest.json?note={id}
If server returns {"profile":{"renderMode":"full","widgetTypes":["custom"],"widgetSink":"script"}} → creator-based, done.

Step 3 — Report to bot:

json
{"url": "/note/{id}/reader"}
The server sets APP.panel = "reader", manifest returns your custom preset → full mode → XSS fires.

Try several custom names: reader, custom, full, embed, share. The panel name just needs to match your readerPresets key AND not be a hardcoded panel.

Read app.js
bash

cat /home/claude/CTF/app.js
Output

(function () {
  'use strict';

  var APP = window.__APP_INIT__ || {};

  var DEFAULTS = {
    maxNoteLength: 50000,
    searchDebounce: 300,
    apiBase: '/api'
  };

  var ACCOUNT_PREFERENCES_API = DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/account/preferences';

  // Settings helpers.

  function mergeFormData(target, source) {
    if (!source || typeof source !== 'object') return target;
    var keys = Object.keys(source);
    for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
      var k = keys[i];
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(source, k)) continue;
      if (typeof source[k] === 'object' && source[k] !== null) continue;
      target[k] = source[k];
    }
    return target;
  }

  function getOwnString(obj, key, fallback) {
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string') {
      return obj[key];
    }
    return fallback;
  }

  function getOwnArray(obj, key) {
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) && Array.isArray(obj[key])) {
      return obj[key];
    }
    return [];
  }

  // Hash-based appearance preferences.

  function setNestedValue(obj, path, value) {
    var keys = path.replace(/\]/g, '').split('[');
    var current = obj;
    for (var i = 0; i < keys.length - 1; i++) {
      var k = keys[i];
      if (k === '__proto__') return;
      if (
        current[k] == null ||
        (typeof current[k] !== 'object' && typeof current[k] !== 'function')
      ) {
        current[k] = {};
      }
      current = current[k];
    }
    var last = keys[keys.length - 1];
    if (last !== '__proto__') {
      current[last] = value;
    }
  }

  function parseThemeParams() {
    var hash = location.hash;
    if (!hash || hash.length < 2) return;
    var raw = hash.substring(1);
    var pairs = raw.split('&');
    var result = {};

    for (var i = 0; i < pairs.length; i++) {
      var idx = pairs[i].indexOf('=');
      if (idx === -1) continue;
      try {
        var key = decodeURIComponent(pairs[i].substring(0, idx));
        var val = decodeURIComponent(pairs[i].substring(idx + 1));
        setNestedValue(result, key, val);
      } catch (e) {
        continue;
      }
    }

    if (result.theme)  APP.theme  = result.theme;
    if (result.font)   document.body.style.fontFamily = result.font;
    if (result.accent) document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent', result.accent);
    if (result.bg)     document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--bg-primary', result.bg);
  }

  // Remote layout manifest.

  function applyRemoteProfile(profile) {
    if (!profile || typeof profile !== 'object') return;

    if (typeof profile.renderMode === 'string') {
      APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode;
    }

    if (Array.isArray(profile.widgetTypes)) {
      APP.widgetTypes = profile.widgetTypes
        .filter(function (value) { return typeof value === 'string'; })
        .slice(0, 8);
    }

    if (typeof profile.widgetSink === 'string') {
      APP.widgetSink = profile.widgetSink;
    }

    if (typeof profile.theme === 'string') {
      APP.theme = profile.theme;
    }
  }

  function loadPanelManifest() {
    if (typeof window.__NOTE_CONTENT__ !== 'string') {
      return Promise.resolve();
    }

    var panel  = typeof APP.panel === 'string' ? APP.panel : 'summary';
    var noteId = typeof APP.noteId === 'string' ? APP.noteId : '';
    if (!noteId) return Promise.resolve();

    var target = '/note/' + encodeURIComponent(noteId) + '/' + panel +
      '/manifest.json?note=' + encodeURIComponent(noteId);

    return fetch(target, {
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    })
      .then(function (r) {
        if (!r.ok) return null;
        return r.json();
      })
      .then(function (data) {
        if (data && data.profile) {
          applyRemoteProfile(data.profile);
        }
      })
      .catch(function () {});
  }

  // Content policies.

  function loadContentPolicies() {
    var mode = getOwnString(APP, 'renderMode', 'safe');
    return {
      allowForms:         mode === 'full',
      allowIds:           mode === 'full',
      allowDataAttrs:     mode === 'full',
      enableEnhancements: mode === 'full'
    };
  }

  // DOMPurify config.

  function getSanitizeConfig() {
    var cfg = {
      ALLOWED_TAGS: [
        'h1','h2','h3','h4','h5','h6',
        'p','br','hr',
        'b','i','u','em','strong','del','ins','sub','sup','mark',
        'a','img',
        'ul','ol','li',
        'blockquote','code','pre','kbd','samp',
        'table','caption','thead','tbody','tfoot','tr','th','td',
        'span','div',
        'figure','figcaption',
        'abbr','cite','q','small','time','var',
        'dl','dt','dd'
      ],
      ALLOWED_ATTR: [
        'href','src','alt','title',
        'class','style',
        'target','rel',
        'width','height',
        'colspan','rowspan','scope',
        'cite','datetime','lang','dir'
      ],
      ALLOW_DATA_ATTR: false
    };

    var policies = loadContentPolicies();

    if (policies.allowForms) {
      cfg.ALLOWED_TAGS = cfg.ALLOWED_TAGS.concat([
        'form','input','select','option','textarea',
        'label','fieldset','legend',
        'details','summary','dialog',
        'meter','progress','output'
      ]);
    }

    if (policies.allowIds) {
      cfg.ALLOWED_ATTR = cfg.ALLOWED_ATTR.concat([
        'id','name','value','type','placeholder',
        'for','method','action',
        'checked','selected','disabled','readonly',
        'required','pattern','autocomplete',
        'rows','cols','wrap','maxlength','minlength',
        'multiple','size','accept','list',
        'open','tabindex','role',
        'min','max','step','low','high','optimum',
        'aria-label','aria-describedby'
      ]);
    }

    if (policies.allowDataAttrs) {
      cfg.ALLOW_DATA_ATTR = true;
    }

    return cfg;
  }

  function sanitize(html) {
    if (typeof DOMPurify === 'undefined') return '';
    return DOMPurify.sanitize(html, getSanitizeConfig());
  }

  // Post-sanitisation data attribute filter.

  var UNSAFE_CONTENT_RE = /script|cookie|document|window|eval|alert|prompt|confirm|Function|fetch|XMLHttp|import|require|setTimeout|setInterval/i;

  function postSanitize(html) {
    var temp = document.createElement('div');
    temp.innerHTML = html;
    temp.querySelectorAll('*').forEach(function (el) {
      var attrs = el.attributes;
      for (var i = attrs.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        var attr = attrs[i];
        if (attr.name.indexOf('data-') === 0 && UNSAFE_CONTENT_RE.test(attr.value)) {
          el.removeAttribute(attr.name);
        }
      }
    });
    return temp.innerHTML;
  }

  // Note rendering.

  function renderNoteContent() {
    var display = document.getElementById('note-display');
    var content = window.__NOTE_CONTENT__;
    if (!display || typeof content !== 'string') return;

    var clean = sanitize(content);
    var safe  = postSanitize(clean);
    display.innerHTML = safe;

    display.querySelectorAll('a[href]').forEach(function (a) {
      if (a.hostname !== location.hostname) {
        a.setAttribute('rel', 'noopener noreferrer');
        a.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
      }
    });

    display.querySelectorAll('img').forEach(function (img) {
      img.loading = 'lazy';
      img.onerror = function () { this.style.display = 'none'; };
    });
  }

  // Inline enhancements.

  function initContentEnhancements() {
    var container = document.getElementById('note-display');
    if (!container) return;

    var observer = new MutationObserver(function () {
      processEnhancements(container);
    });
    observer.observe(container, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  }

  function processEnhancements(root) {
    var policies = loadContentPolicies();
    if (!policies.enableEnhancements) return;

    var manifestTypes = getOwnArray(APP, 'widgetTypes');
    if (!manifestTypes.length) return;

    var configEl = document.getElementById('enhance-config');
    if (!configEl) return;
    var allowedTypes = (configEl.dataset.types || '').split(',');

    root.querySelectorAll('[data-enhance]:not([data-processed])').forEach(function (el) {
      el.dataset.processed = '1';
      var type = el.dataset.enhance;
      if (allowedTypes.indexOf(type) === -1) return;
      if (manifestTypes.indexOf(type) === -1) return;

      switch (type) {
        case 'counter':
          animateCounter(el);
          break;
        case 'progress':
          animateProgress(el);
          break;
        case 'custom':
          loadCustomWidget(el);
          break;
      }
    });
  }

  function animateCounter(el) {
    var target = parseInt(el.dataset.to || '100', 10);
    var current = 0;
    var step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(target / 60));
    var timer = setInterval(function () {
      current = Math.min(current + step, target);
      el.textContent = current;
      if (current >= target) clearInterval(timer);
    }, 16);
  }

  function animateProgress(el) {
    var pct = parseInt(el.dataset.pct || '0', 10);
    el.style.width = '0%';
    el.style.transition = 'width 1s ease';
    requestAnimationFrame(function () {
      el.style.width = Math.min(pct, 100) + '%';
    });
  }

  function loadCustomWidget(el) {
    if (getOwnString(APP, 'widgetSink', 'text') !== 'script') return;

    var cfg = el.dataset.cfg;
    if (!cfg || cfg.length > 512) return;
    var s = document.createElement('script');
    s.textContent = cfg;
    document.head.appendChild(s);
  }

  // Search.

  var searchTimer = null;

  function initSearch() {
    var input   = document.getElementById('search-input');
    var results = document.getElementById('search-results');
    if (!input || !results) return;

    input.addEventListener('input', function () {
      clearTimeout(searchTimer);
      var q = this.value.trim();
      if (q.length < 2) { results.innerHTML = ''; return; }

      searchTimer = setTimeout(function () {
        fetch(DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent(q))
          .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
          .then(function (data) {
            if (!data.results || !data.results.length) {
              results.innerHTML = '<div class="no-results">No notes found</div>';
              return;
            }
            results.innerHTML = data.results.map(function (n) {
              return '<a href="/note/' + encodeURIComponent(n.id) +
                     '" class="search-result">' + escapeHtml(n.title) + '</a>';
            }).join('');
          })
          .catch(function () {
            results.innerHTML = '<div class="no-results">Search failed</div>';
          });
      }, DEFAULTS.searchDebounce);
    });
  }

  // Local note history.

  var STORAGE_KEY = 'chainnotes_my_ids';

  function getSavedIds() {
    try {
      var raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
      if (!raw) return [];
      var ids = JSON.parse(raw);
      return Array.isArray(ids) ? ids : [];
    } catch (e) {
      return [];
    }
  }

  function saveNoteId(id) {
    var ids = getSavedIds();
    if (ids.indexOf(id) === -1) {
      ids.unshift(id);
      if (ids.length > 200) ids = ids.slice(0, 200);
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(ids));
    }
  }

  function loadPrivateNotes() {
    var grid  = document.getElementById('private-notes-grid');
    var empty = document.getElementById('private-notes-empty');
    if (!grid) return;

    var ids = getSavedIds();
    if (!ids.length) return;

    fetch(DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/notes/lookup', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ ids: ids })
    })
      .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
      .then(function (data) {
        if (!data.notes) return;
        var found = data.notes.filter(function (n) { return n.found; });
        if (!found.length) return;
        if (empty) empty.style.display = 'none';
        found.forEach(function (n) {
          var a = document.createElement('a');
          a.href = '/note/' + encodeURIComponent(n.id);
          a.className = 'note-card';
          var h3 = document.createElement('h3');
          h3.textContent = n.title;
          var span = document.createElement('span');
          span.className = 'note-card-author';
          span.textContent = n.author;
          a.appendChild(h3);
          a.appendChild(span);
          grid.appendChild(a);
        });
      })
      .catch(function () {});
  }

  // Note creation.

  function initCreateForm() {
    var form   = document.getElementById('create-form');
    var result = document.getElementById('create-result');
    if (!form) return;

    form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var title   = form.querySelector('[name="title"]').value.trim();
      var content = form.querySelector('[name="content"]').value;

      if (!title || !content) {
        showResult(result, 'error', 'Title and content are required.');
        return;
      }

      fetch(DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/notes', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ title: title, content: content })
      })
        .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function (data) {
          if (data.success) {
            saveNoteId(data.id);
            showResult(result, 'success',
              'Note created! <a href="' + escapeHtml(data.url) + '">View note &rarr;</a>');
            form.reset();
            loadPrivateNotes();
          } else {
            showResult(result, 'error', data.error || 'Failed to create note.');
          }
        })
        .catch(function () {
          showResult(result, 'error', 'Network error.');
        });
    });
  }

  // Settings.

  function loadAccountPreferences() {
    var form = document.getElementById('settings-form');
    var meta = document.getElementById('settings-meta');

    return fetch(ACCOUNT_PREFERENCES_API)
      .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
      .then(function (data) {
        if (!data || !data.preferences) return;

        if (form) {
          setFieldValue(form, 'theme', data.preferences.theme);
          setFieldValue(form, 'fontSize', data.preferences.fontSize);
          setFieldValue(form, 'language', data.preferences.language);
          setFieldValue(form, 'defaultLayout', data.preferences.defaultLayout);
        }

        if (meta) {
          var presetCount = data.stats && typeof data.stats.presetCount === 'number'
            ? data.stats.presetCount
            : 0;
          meta.textContent = presetCount
            ? presetCount + ' reader preset' + (presetCount === 1 ? '' : 's') + ' synced to this account.'
            : 'Reader presets sync to this account automatically when they are created.';
        }
      })
      .catch(function () {});
  }

  function initSettingsForm() {
    var form   = document.getElementById('settings-form');
    var result = document.getElementById('settings-result');
    if (!form) return;

    form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var payload = {};
      new FormData(form).forEach(function (v, k) {
        payload[k] = isNaN(v) ? v : Number(v);
      });

      var merged = {};
      mergeFormData(merged, payload);

      fetch(ACCOUNT_PREFERENCES_API, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(merged)
      })
        .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function (data) {
          if (data.success) {
            if (data.preferences && typeof data.preferences.theme === 'string') {
              APP.theme = data.preferences.theme;
              applyTheme();
            }
            loadAccountPreferences();
            showResult(result, 'success', 'Settings saved.');
          } else {
            showResult(result, 'error', data.error || 'Failed.');
          }
        })
        .catch(function () {
          showResult(result, 'error', 'Network error.');
        });
    });
  }

  // Review request.

  function initReportButton() {
    var btn    = document.getElementById('report-btn');
    var result = document.getElementById('report-result');
    if (!btn) return;

    btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
      btn.disabled = true;
      var url = location.pathname + location.search + location.hash;

      fetch(DEFAULTS.apiBase + '/report', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ url: url })
      })
        .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
        .then(function (data) {
          showResult(result, data.success || data.message ? 'success' : 'error',
            data.message || data.error);
          setTimeout(function () { btn.disabled = false; }, 10000);
        })
        .catch(function () {
          showResult(result, 'error', 'Network error.');
          btn.disabled = false;
        });
    });
  }

  // Theme.

  function applyTheme() {
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', APP.theme || 'dark');
  }

  // Utilities.

  function setFieldValue(form, name, value) {
    var field = form.querySelector('[name="' + name + '"]');
    if (!field || value == null) return;
    field.value = value;
  }

  function escapeHtml(str) {
    var d = document.createElement('div');
    d.textContent = str;
    return d.innerHTML;
  }

  function showResult(el, type, msg) {
    if (!el) return;
    el.className = 'result-msg result-' + type;
    el.innerHTML = msg;
    el.style.display = 'block';
    setTimeout(function () { el.style.display = 'none'; }, 8000);
  }

  // Init.

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async function () {
    parseThemeParams();
    await loadPanelManifest();
    applyTheme();
    initContentEnhancements();
    renderNoteContent();
    initSearch();
    initCreateForm();
    initSettingsForm();
    initReportButton();
    loadPrivateNotes();
    loadAccountPreferences();
  });
})();

Decode key responses from New.xml
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
import base64

tree = ET.parse('/mnt/user-data/uploads/New.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

# Look at the full URLs to see panels, and decode interesting responses
for i in [3, 11, 14, 17, 20, 30, 31, 41, 42, 44, 45, 47]:
    item = items[i]
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    # decode response
    resp_el = item.find('response')
    if resp_el is not None and resp_el.get('base64') == 'true':
        try:
            resp = base64.b64decode(resp_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
        except:
            resp = resp_el.text or ''
    else:
        resp = resp_el.text if resp_el is not None else ''
    
    # Show URL and first 300 chars of response body (after headers)
    body_start = resp.find('\r\n\r\n')
    body = resp[body_start+4:body_start+500] if body_start != -1 else resp[:500]
    print(f'=== [{i}] {status} {url[-80:]}')
    print(body[:300])
    print()
"

javascript
function applyRemoteProfile(profile) {
    if (!profile || typeof profile !== 'object') return;

    if (typeof profile.renderMode === 'string') {
      APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode;  // Sets to "safe"
    }
    // ...
}
And loadContentPolicies:

javascript
function loadContentPolicies() {
    var mode = getOwnString(APP, 'renderMode', 'safe');
    return {
      allowForms:         mode === 'full',
      allowIds:           mode === 'full',
      allowDataAttrs:     mode === 'full',
      enableEnhancements: mode === 'full'
    };
}
getOwnString uses hasOwnProperty, so prototype pollution on renderMode won't work.

But wait - applyRemoteProfile directly sets APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode. If we can control what the manifest returns...

Find all manifest requests and their panels
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
import base64

tree = ET.parse('/mnt/user-data/uploads/New.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

# Find all manifest requests and show their full URLs and responses
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    if 'manifest' in url:
        status = item.findtext('status','')
        resp_el = item.find('response')
        if resp_el is not None and resp_el.get('base64') == 'true':
            resp = base64.b64decode(resp_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
        else:
            resp = resp_el.text if resp_el is not None else ''
        body_start = resp.find('\r\n\r\n')
        body = resp[body_start+4:body_start+300] if body_start != -1 else resp[:300]
        # also get request
        req_el = item.find('request')
        if req_el is not None and req_el.get('base64') == 'true':
            req = base64.b64decode(req_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
        else:
            req = req_el.text if req_el is not None else ''
        print(f'=== [{i}] {status} {url}')
        print('REQ first line:', req.split('\n')[0])
        print('RESP:', body[:200])
        print()
"

Let me re-read app.js very carefully.

The init sequence is:

javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async function () {
    parseThemeParams();           // 1. reads URL hash
    await loadPanelManifest();    // 2. fetches manifest, calls applyRemoteProfile
    applyTheme();                 // 3.
    initContentEnhancements();    // 4. sets up MutationObserver
    renderNoteContent();          // 5. renders note content
    ...
});
applyRemoteProfile sets APP.renderMode directly. If the manifest returns "safe", then APP.renderMode = "safe".

loadContentPolicies() uses getOwnString(APP, 'renderMode', 'safe') with hasOwnProperty. So APP.renderMode is checked as an own property.

Wait. What if applyRemoteProfile is called with a profile where profile.renderMode is truthy but not 'full'? That sets APP.renderMode = "safe".

What if applyRemoteProfile is NOT called at all? Then APP.renderMode is never set as own property, so getOwnString returns 'safe' as fallback.

Hmm. Is there any way to get APP.renderMode set to 'full' as an OWN property?

Only applyRemoteProfile sets APP.renderMode (as APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode). And the server always returns "safe".

Check API responses and account preferences
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
import base64

tree = ET.parse('/mnt/user-data/uploads/New.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

# Check lookup, search, and any other API endpoints
for i in [21, 46, 47]:
    item = items[i]
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    resp_el = item.find('response')
    if resp_el.get('base64') == 'true':
        resp = base64.b64decode(resp_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    else:
        resp = resp_el.text or ''
    body_start = resp.find('\r\n\r\n')
    body = resp[body_start+4:body_start+500] if body_start != -1 else resp[:500]
    
    req_el = item.find('request')
    if req_el.get('base64') == 'true':
        req = base64.b64decode(req_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    else:
        req = req_el.text or ''
    req_body_start = req.find('\r\n\r\n')
    req_body = req[req_body_start+4:req_body_start+300] if req_body_start != -1 else ''
    
    print(f'[{i}] {method} {status} {url}')
    print('REQ:', req_body[:200])
    print('RESP:', body[:300])
    print()

# Also check account prefs 200 response from CTF.xml
tree2 = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/CTF.xml')
root2 = tree2.getroot()
items2 = root2.findall('.//item')
for i, item in enumerate(items2):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    if 'account/preferences' in url and status == '200':
        resp_el = item.find('response')
        if resp_el is not None and resp_el.get('base64') == 'true':
            resp = base64.b64decode(resp_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
        else:
            resp = resp_el.text or ''
        body_start = resp.find('\r\n\r\n')
        body = resp[body_start+4:body_start+500] if body_start != -1 else resp[:500]
        print(f'CTF.xml [{i}] account/prefs 200:', body[:300])
        break
"

The question is: is there ANY way to get APP.renderMode = "full" as an own property?

Let me look at this from a completely different angle. What if the key is NOT about the manifest at all, but about a different path?

Actually wait. Let me re-read loadContentPolicies:

javascript
function loadContentPolicies() {
    var mode = getOwnString(APP, 'renderMode', 'safe');
    return {
      allowForms:         mode === 'full',
      allowIds:           mode === 'full',
      allowDataAttrs:     mode === 'full',
      enableEnhancements: mode === 'full'
    };
}
getOwnString is called with APP. APP = window.__APP_INIT__ || {}. After applyRemoteProfile, APP.renderMode = "safe" (own property).

What if we pollute Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty? That would break Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) check!

getOwnString does:

javascript
if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) && typeof obj[key] === 'string') {
    return obj[key];
}
If we set Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty to something... Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call would fail or behave differently.

But setting Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty = function() { return true; } via prototype pollution wouldn't work because Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty is already own on Object.prototype. We'd need to REPLACE it.

Actually, setNestedValue(result, 'constructor[prototype][hasOwnProperty]', 'anything') would set Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty = 'anything'. Then Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key) would throw TypeError: Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call is not a function.

Find all preferences requests in old CTF.xml
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
import base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/CTF.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

# Find account/preferences POST and 200 GET responses
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    if 'account/preferences' in url:
        resp_el = item.find('response')
        if resp_el is not None:
            if resp_el.get('base64') == 'true':
                resp = base64.b64decode(resp_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
            else:
                resp = resp_el.text or ''
            body_start = resp.find('\r\n\r\n')
            body = resp[body_start+4:body_start+600] if body_start != -1 else resp[:600]
            
            req_el = item.find('request')
            if req_el is not None:
                if req_el.get('base64') == 'true':
                    req = base64.b64decode(req_el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
                else:
                    req = req_el.text or ''
                req_body_start = req.find('\r\n\r\n')
                req_body = req[req_body_start+4:req_body_start+400] if req_body_start != -1 else ''
            else:
                req_body = ''
            
            print(f'[{i}] {method} {status} {url}')
            if req_body.strip(): print('REQ:', req_body)
            print('RESP:', body[:400])
            print()
"

json
{"theme":"dark","fontSize":14,"language":"en","defaultLayout":"summary"}
If we POST:

json

The server might accept and store this. Then when the manifest is requested for our note, it returns the preset data with renderMode: "full".

Actually, I realize we need to be smarter. mergeFormData skips objects (if (typeof source[k] === 'object' && source[k] !== null) continue;). So readerPresets (which is an object) would be skipped by mergeFormData.

But we're POSTing directly! We don't go through the client-side mergeFormData.

OR: POST readerPresets with renderMode: full using the INCOGNITO session, then visit the manifest with the incognito session. If it returns full, then it's visitor-based.

The user is saying "I opened the note in incognito" - showing the manifest returns safe for a fresh session. This suggests we need to investigate further.

But wait - the widgetTypes: ["counter", "progress"] in the incognito manifest response is interesting. The incognito session has readerPresets: {} (empty). But the manifest returns widgetTypes: ["counter", "progress"].

This is a contradiction! If readerPresets is empty, why does the manifest have non-empty widgetTypes?

This strongly suggests the manifest is NOT based on the visitor's readerPresets, but rather on the note creator's presets or some server-side default.

Decode all New1.xml items fully
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET, base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/New1.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

def decode(el):
    if el is None: return ''
    if el.get('base64') == 'true': return base64.b64decode(el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    return el.text or ''

def body(s):
    i = s.find('\r\n\r\n')
    return s[i+4:] if i != -1 else s

# Show all requests/responses with full detail
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    req = decode(item.find('request'))
    resp = decode(item.find('response'))
    req_body = body(req)
    resp_body = body(resp)
    print(f'=== [{i}] {method} {status} {url}')
    if req_body.strip(): print('REQ:', req_body[:400])
    print('RESP:', resp_body[:500])
    print()
"

Check which session cookie each request uses
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET, base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/New1.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

def decode(el):
    if el is None: return ''
    if el.get('base64') == 'true': return base64.b64decode(el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    return el.text or ''

# Check cookies on ALL requests to see which session is which
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    req = decode(item.find('request'))
    # find Cookie header
    for line in req.split('\r\n'):
        if line.lower().startswith('cookie:'):
            print(f'[{i}] {method} {url[-60:]}')
            print('  Cookie:', line)
            break
"

Same session. Full prefs. Manifest safe. This means: readerPresets have absolutely no effect on the manifest endpoint.

Sort by timestamp to get true chronological order
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET, base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/New1.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

# Print ALL items with timestamps, sorted by time
import re
data = []
for i, item in enumerate(items):
    t = item.findtext('time','')
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    data.append((t, i, method, status, url))

for t, i, method, status, url in sorted(data):
    print(f'{t} [{i}] {method} {status} {url[-70:]}')
"

function processEnhancements(root) {

  if (!policies.enableEnhancements) return;  // ← gated by renderMode: full

loadContentPolicies checks mode === 'full' for everything. There's no way around this.

Look at applyRemoteProfile:

js
if (typeof profile.renderMode === 'string') {
  APP.renderMode = profile.renderMode;  // only runs if own property!
}
If profile has NO own renderMode, profile.renderMode resolves via prototype chain. If we've polluted Object.prototype.renderMode = 'full' → APP.renderMode = 'full' gets set as OWN property → getOwnString finds it ✓

The two-part attack:

Part 1 — Set readerPresets WITHOUT renderMode (only widgetTypes + widgetSink):

json
{
  "readerPresets": {
    "summary": {
      "widgetTypes": ["custom"],
      "widgetSink": "script"
    }
  }
}
If the server applies your preset to the manifest profile but omits renderMode (since you didn't set it), the manifest returns {profile: {widgetTypes: ["custom"], widgetSink: "script"}} — no own renderMode.

Part 2 — Prototype pollution in the hash URL you report to bot:

/note/{id}/summary#constructor[prototype][renderMode]=full
Flow on bot's page:

parseThemeParams() → Object.prototype.renderMode = 'full'
loadPanelManifest() → manifest returns {profile: {widgetTypes:["custom"], widgetSink:"script"}} ← no renderMode
applyRemoteProfile(profile) → typeof profile.renderMode === 'string' → checks prototype → 'full' → APP.renderMode = 'full' ✓
DOMPurify allows data-attrs → widget fires → flag stolen
Test now in Burp Repeater: POST readerPresets WITHOUT renderMode, then fresh manifest fetch. Does it return {profile: {widgetTypes: ["custom"], widgetSink: "script"}} with no renderMode?

Decode key items with timestamps and cookies
bash

python3 -c "
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET, base64

tree = ET.parse('/home/claude/CTF/804576bc8115ce7477895a776ca331f0.xml')
root = tree.getroot()
items = root.findall('.//item')

def decode(el):
    if el is None: return ''
    if el.get('base64') == 'true': return base64.b64decode(el.text).decode('utf-8', errors='replace')
    return el.text or ''
def body(s):
    i = s.find('\r\n\r\n')
    return s[i+4:] if i != -1 else s
def cookie(s):
    for line in s.split('\r\n'):
        if line.lower().startswith('cookie:'): return line[8:].strip()
    return ''

# Focus on key items sorted by time
key = [18, 10, 4, 9, 3, 2, 0]
for i in key:
    item = items[i]
    t = item.findtext('time','')
    url = item.findtext('url','')
    method = item.findtext('method','')
    status = item.findtext('status','')
    req = decode(item.find('request'))
    resp = decode(item.find('response'))
    req_body = body(req)
    resp_body = body(resp)
    ck = cookie(req)
    print(f'=== [{i}] {t} | {method} {status}')
    print(f'    URL: {url[-80:]}')
    print(f'    Cookie: {ck[:60]}')
    if req_body.strip(): print(f'    REQ: {req_body[:300]}')
    print(f'    RESP: {resp_body[:400]}')
    print()
"

    url = e['request']['url']
    method = e['request']['method']

        print(f'[{i}] POST preferences found!')

    url = e['request']['url']
    if 'manifest' in url:
        print(f'[{i}] Manifest: {url}')
        # Check all query params
        for p in e['request'].get('queryString', []):
            print(f'  param: {p}')
        # Full response
        txt = e['response']['content'].get('text','')
        print(f'  RESP: {txt}')

# Also check the note page for APP_INIT
e = entries[31]
txt = e['response']['content'].get('text','')
idx = txt.find('APP_INIT')
if idx >= 0:
    print('APP_INIT:', txt[idx-5:idx+300])
"

Key observation: The manifest request at [37] has NO COOKIE in the request headers! The cookie is completely missing from the manifest request.

Look at the headers - there's no cookie: header. The request is made without a session cookie.

This is the key insight! The manifest request from the page's loadPanelManifest() is a fetch() call:

js
return fetch(target, {
    headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
})
This fetch() call doesn't include credentials: 'include' or any credentials option. In browsers, the default for fetch() is credentials: 'same-origin'. Wait, actually the default changed. In older specs it was 'omit', but in modern browsers (and Fetch spec) the default is 'same-origin' which includes cookies for same-origin requests.

But looking at the request - there's no cookie! So either:

The fetch is being made with credentials: 'omit'
Or the user opened the note page in incognito where they had no session cookie
Wait, but the HAR file is named after the session 804576bc8115ce7477895a776ca331f0, so it should be a logged-in session.

But look at the request headers more carefully - there's NO :authority + cookie combo. No cookie at all. But the account preferences request right before/after DO have the session cookie (since they're triggered by the page's loadAccountPreferences which also uses fetch but DOES include cookies).

Actually I think the issue is that the HAR captures might not include cookies in the headers (some browsers redact them for privacy). Let me look at this differently.

No nesting-based depth checks in the min.js. This is consistent with DOMPurify 3.4.0 which removed nesting-based mXSS protection.
The purify.ts has SAFE_FOR_TEMPLATES = false by default, and FORCE_BODY = false. The app.js doesn't set these in getSanitizeConfig(), so they default to false/no effect.
Let me try a completely different approach and look for mXSS possibilities in the app itself.
One thing I noticed: renderNoteContent does:
jsvar clean = sanitize(content);
var safe  = postSanitize(clean);
display.innerHTML = safe;
The postSanitize uses:
jsfunction postSanitize(html) {
    var temp = document.createElement('div');
    temp.innerHTML = html;
    ...
    return temp.innerHTML;
}
There's a double innerHTML parse! First DOMPurify sanitizes and produces a string. Then postSanitize does temp.innerHTML = html (parsing again) and returns temp.innerHTML. Then display.innerHTML = safe parses a THIRD time.
This double-parse can lead to mXSS! If the DOMPurify output has content that when parsed a second time produces different HTML.
Wait, actually this is the classic mXSS problem. DOMPurify sanitizes once (safe), but when the safe output is re-parsed by postSanitize's temp.innerHTML = html, it might change. Then display.innerHTML = temp.innerHTML might produce unsafe HTML.
But DOMPurify 3.4.0 should protect against this. Unless there's a specific case that's not covered.
Actually, let me think about what the ALLOWED_TAGS includes: 'table','caption','thead','tbody','tfoot','tr','th','td'. Tables are interesting for mXSS because browsers have specific rules about table content.
Let me look at potential mXSS vectors with the specific ALLOWED_TAGS and ALLOWED_ATTR list.
The style attribute is allowed. CSS injection via style attribute is possible (but probably not useful for XSS given the CSP).
